Int, xs: List[Int]): List[Int] = {\n        val (l, r) = xs.span(_ > x)\n        if (l.isEmpty) r.reverse ++ List(x)\n        else l.last :: (l.init ++ List(x) ++ r).reverse\n    }\n\n    def
